                        <div data-reactid="1091">
                         I rent a separate guesthouse, a little house in my garden with a separate entrance. It consists of one room with a king-size bed and a separate bathroom. Beside my separate guesthouse you can rent a suite in my house, also with a king-size bed and a separate bathroom. My house is located nearby a lagoon, 100m distance. It has a friendly, sunny garden, with a small terrace, where you can take your breakfast. The Lagoon of Araruama is well known for its warm waters and its high salinity, one of the largest lagoon in the world!. It has one of the largest wind streaks in the country. It’s a really paradise for kite surfers! You’ll find a kite surfers school next to my house. The distance of my house to Rio de Janeiro is 100 km, to the next bigger city – Araruama - is 7 km and to Cabo Frio and Búzios appr. 50 km. It takes 2 hours by car from the international Airport Galeão in Rio (GIG) to my house. From the Airport in Rio de Janeiro you can take a bus to Niterói or to Araruama and from there also a bus, direction Cabo Frio (the station where you have to get off is called LAKE VIEW), or you take a taxi from Araruama directly to my house. In any case I'm always available for my guests with my local knowledge and language skills e. g. to rent a car, to do shopping, to search for medical care, to give tips for trips, etc. If it is required I can also teach portuguese for foreigners. By request I can prepare a special dinner for you. I am cooking international and vegetarian food also with regard to the breakfast. The price includes a rich breakfast with fresh fruits and fresh juice, homemade bread, cake and jams. As far as possible I use organic products from the region. I don’t have TV, but wireless internet (WiFi). I'm ayurvedic therapist and offer massage, shirodhara and consultation.

                         Linda casa, 3 quartos sendo 2 suítes perto da lagoa (900m) e de todo o centro (1,5km) de Araruama. Em volta das praias mais lindas da Região dos Lagos. Área de lazer com piscina e espaço gourmet. Perfeito para temporadas com a família e amigos.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1404">
                         A casa é composta por 2 salas: sendo uma de jantar no mesmo ambiente, uma sala de estar. 3 quartos, sendo 2 suítes: a suíte master tem uma cama de casal, ar condicionado, um closet e banheiro; a outra suíte de solteiro (1 cama de solteiro), com ar condicionado, armário; o outro quarto tem uma cama de casal, armário e ventilador de teto. Na área de lazer tem piscina rasa, mesas e cadeiras, churrasqueira e forno/fogão (com todos os utensílios para usa-las) a lenha. 3 vagas na garagem.
                        </div>
